# global order_date
# order_date = " {{ dag_run.conf['order_date'] }} "

def get_filter_string(servicename, country):
    filter_service_dict = {"TRD-GPTM-FSDP": country_dict,
                           "PRTY_TRD_RLTD-GPTM-FSDP": country_dict,
                           "SUB_LDGR-FPSL-GPTM-ACTG": country_dict,
                           "ALT_TRD-GPTM-FSDP": country_dict,
                           "SUBL_PEBAL_COA_RECON-GPTM-ACCT_BS": country_dict,
                           "SUB_LDGR-FPSL-GPTM-ACTG_PL": country_dict,
						   "SUB_LDGR_TRD_RLTD-GPTM-TRADE_PL" : country_dict
                           }
    if servicename in filter_service_dict and country in country_dict:
        filter_str = "dummy"  # "CTRY_CD=" + filter_service_dict[servicename][country]
    else:
        filter_str = "dummy"
    return filter_str


def update_params():
    global order_date
    order_date = " {{ dag_run.conf['order_date'] }} "
    order_date = order_date.strip()
    # " {{ dag_run.conf['order_date'] }} "
    print("========================> AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA " + order_date + "" + "daeeeeeeee")


def get_all_services_set():
    services_list = []
    for k, v in product_services_ingestion_dict.items():
        for s, i in v.items():
            services_list.append(s)
    return set(services_list)


def get_all_ingestion_tables_set():
    ingestion_tables_list = []
    for prd, serv_dict in product_services_ingestion_dict.items():
        for serv, ing_str in serv_dict.items():
            ingestion_tables_list_all = ing_str.split(",")
            for ing_tab in ingestion_tables_list_all:
                if ing_tab not in services_set:
                    if ing_tab not in products_set:
                        ingestion_tables_list.append(ing_tab)
    return set(ingestion_tables_list)


products_set = product_services_ingestion_dict.keys()
services_set = get_all_services_set()
ing_set = get_all_ingestion_tables_set()

tasks_dict = {}


def create_ing_tasks():
    for ing_tab in ing_set:
        table_id = ingestion_table_name_to_id_dict[ing_tab.strip()]
        ing_tab_params_arr = ing_tab_id_to_params_map[table_id].split(",")
        source = ing_tab_params_arr[0]
        country = ing_tab_params_arr[1]
        tp = ing_tab_params_arr[2]
        print("===========" + ing_tab + "============")
        print('sh -x /CTRLFW/FDP/{0}/ingestion/scripts/fdp_staging_loader.sh {1} {2} {3}'.format(env,
                                                                                                 order_date,
                                                                                                 env,
                                                                                                 table_id))
        ing_tab_task = BashOperator(task_id="Ingestion_" + ing_tab + "_" + env,
                                    bash_command='sh -x /CTRLFW/FDP/{0}/ingestion/scripts/fdp_staging_loader.sh {1} {2} {3}'.format(
                                        env, order_date, env, table_id), dag=dag,
                                    execution_timeout=timedelta(hours=20))

        tasks_dict[ing_tab] = ing_tab_task


serv_to_prod_dict = {}


def build_serv_to_prod_dict():
    for p, sd in product_services_ingestion_dict.items():
        for s, i in sd.items():
            serv_to_prod_dict[s] = p


def get_part_col_to_val_dict(service_param_str, filter_clause):
    filter_clause_map = build_map_with_filter_clause(filter_clause)
    part_col_to_val_or_var_map = {}
    part_vars_arr = service_param_str.split(";")
    for part_var in part_vars_arr:
        part_to_val_or_var = part_var.split("=")
        part_col_val = part_to_val_or_var[1]
        if part_to_val_or_var[1] in filter_clause_map:
            part_col_val = filter_clause_map[part_col_val]
            if part_col_val in country_dict:
                part_col_val = country_dict[part_col_val]
        part_col_to_val_or_var_map[part_to_val_or_var[0]] = part_col_val
        print("Getting the partition col to val map".format(str(part_col_to_val_or_var_map)))
    return part_col_to_val_or_var_map


def build_map_with_filter_clause(filter_clause):
    filter_clause_map = {}
    filter_vars_arr = filter_clause.split(";")
    for filter_var in filter_vars_arr:
        filter_col_to_val = filter_var.split("=")
        if len(filter_col_to_val) == 2:
            filter_clause_map[filter_col_to_val[0]] = filter_col_to_val[1]
    return filter_clause_map


def create_dq_task(service, service_param_str, product_name, filter_clause):
    part_col_to_val_dict = get_part_col_to_val_dict(service_param_str, filter_clause)
    dq_ods_val = part_col_to_val_dict["ods_val"]
    dq_country_val = part_col_to_val_dict["country_val"]
    dq_tp_val = part_col_to_val_dict["tp_sys_val"]
    dq_process_id_val = part_col_to_val_dict["process_id_val"]

    print(" DQ job command for service {0} for product {1}".format(service, product_name))
    print(
        "sh -x /CTRLFW/FDP/{0}/dq/fdp_dq_trigger.sh {1} {2} {3} {4} {5} {6}".format(env, env, product_name, dq_ods_val,
                                                                                    dq_country_val, dq_tp_val,
                                                                                    dq_process_id_val))
    dq_service_task = BashOperator(task_id="dq_" + service + "_" + env,
                                   bash_command="sh -x /CTRLFW/FDP/{0}/dq/fdp_dq_trigger.sh {1} {2} {3} {4} {5} {6}".format(
                                       env, env, product_name, dq_ods_val, dq_country_val, dq_tp_val,
                                       dq_process_id_val), dag=dag, execution_timeout=timedelta(hours=20))

    tasks_dict["dq_" + service] = dq_service_task


def create_service_tasks():
    for service in services_set:
        service_param_str_with_var = service_params_dict[service]
        service_param_str = service_param_str_with_var.replace("${ods_val_param}", order_date)
        product_name = serv_to_prod_dict[service]
        filter_str = get_filter_string(service, 'NA')
        print("==============" + service + "=========== product " + product_name)
        print("sh -x /CTRLFW/FDP/{0}/daas/pyspark_scripts/fdp_daas_new_version.sh {1} {2} {3} {4} {5} '{6}' '$7'".format(env,
                                                                                                                    env,
                                                                                                                    order_date,
                                                                                                                    product_name,
                                                                                                                    service,
                                                                                                                    'ALL',
                                                                                                                    service_param_str,
                                                                                                                    ''))
        prod_tab_task = BashOperator(task_id="product_" + service + "_" + env,
                                     bash_command="sh -x /CTRLFW/FDP/{0}/daas/pyspark_scripts/fdp_daas_new_version.sh {1} {2} {3} {4} {5} '{6}' {7} {8} ".format(
                                         env, env, order_date, product_name, service, 'ALL', service_param_str,
                                         filter_str, "daily"), dag=dag, execution_timeout=timedelta(hours=20))

        create_dq_task(service, service_param_str, product_name, filter_str)

        tasks_dict[service] = prod_tab_task


countries_str = "GBR,HKG,JER,SGP,MYS,BHR,BWA,JPN,KEN,MAC,MUS,OMN,PAK,QAT,SAU,ZMB,ARE,AGO,CIV,CMR,GHA,GMB,IRQ,JOR,NGA,SLE,TZA,UGA,ZAF,ZWE,VNM,TWN,THA,LKA,IDN,BGD,PHL,NPL,BRN,DFC,IND,CHN,KOR,DEU,USA"  # countries_str = "GBR,HKG,JER,SGP,MYS,QAT,OMN,BHR,SAU,MAC"

country_prod_service_dict = {
    "TRD": {"TRD-GPTM-FSDP": "FSDP_GPT_<country_cd>_FINANCIAL_CONTRACT,M_CDL_GLBU_TO_ENTCD_BKCD_XLATE,M_PRODUCT_XLATE"},
    "PRTY_TRD_RLTD": {"PRTY_TRD_RLTD-GPTM-FSDP": "FSDP_GPT_<country_cd>_FINANCIAL_CONTRACT"},
    "SUB_LDGR": {"SUB_LDGR-FPSL-GPTM-ACTG": "FPSL_GPT_<country_cd>_ACCOUNTING_BS", "SUB_LDGR-FPSL-GPTM-ACTG_PL": "FPSL_GPT_<country_cd>_ACCOUNTING_PL"},
    "ALT_TRD": {"ALT_TRD-GPTM-FSDP": "FSDP_GPT_<country_cd>_FINANCIAL_CONTRACT"},
	"SUB_LDGR_TRD_RLTD": {"SUB_LDGR_TRD_RLTD-GPTM-TRADE_PL": "FPSL_GPT_<country_cd>_ACCOUNTING_PL"}
}


def build_country_specific_dependencies():
    for country in countries_str.split(","):
        print(" BBB Processing the country " + country)
        for product_name, country_service_dict in country_prod_service_dict.items():
            print("BBB processing product {0}  country {1}".format(product_name, country))
            start_prod_name = "start_" + product_name
            if product_name not in tasks_dict:
                prod_task = EmptyOperator(task_id='{0}_{1}'.format(product_name, env))
                tasks_dict[product_name] = prod_task
            if start_prod_name not in tasks_dict:
                start_prod_task = EmptyOperator(task_id='{0}_{1}_{2}'.format("start", product_name, env))
                tasks_dict[start_prod_name] = start_prod_task
            for service_name, ing_str in country_service_dict.items():
                # country_service_name = service_name + "_" + country
                country_service_name = service_name
                print(
                    "AAAAAA processing {0} product {1} country {2} service".format(product_name, country, service_name))
                service_param_str_with_var = service_params_dict[service_name]
                service_param_str = service_param_str_with_var.replace("${ods_val_param}", order_date)
                # product_name = serv_to_prod_dict[service_name]
                if country_service_name not in tasks_dict:
                    print("==============" + service_name + "=========== product " + product_name)
                    filter_str = get_filter_string(service_name, country)
                    print(
                        "sh -x /CTRLFW/FDP/{0}/daas/pyspark_scripts/fdp_daas_new.sh {1} {2} {3} {4} {5} '{6}' {7}".format(
                            env, env, order_date, product_name, service_name, 'ALL', service_param_str, filter_str))
                    prod_tab_task = BashOperator(task_id="product_" + country_service_name + "_" + env,
                                                 bash_command="sh -x /CTRLFW/FDP/{0}/daas/pyspark_scripts/fdp_daas_new_version.sh {1} {2} {3} {4} {5} '{6}' {7} {8}".format(
                                                     env, env, order_date, product_name, service_name, 'ALL',
                                                     service_param_str, filter_str, 'daily'), dag=dag,
                                                 execution_timeout=timedelta(hours=20))
                    create_dq_task(country_service_name, service_param_str, product_name, filter_str)
                    tasks_dict[country_service_name] = prod_tab_task

                for ing_tab_ctr in ing_str.split(","):
                    ing_tab = ing_tab_ctr.replace("<country_cd>", country)
                    table_id = ingestion_table_name_to_id_dict[ing_tab.strip()]
                    ing_tab_params_arr = ing_tab_id_to_params_map[table_id].split(",")
                    source = ing_tab_params_arr[0]
                    country_ing = ing_tab_params_arr[1]
                    tp = ing_tab_params_arr[2]
                    print("===========" + ing_tab + "============")
                    if ing_tab not in tasks_dict:
                        print('sh -x /CTRLFW/FDP/{0}/ingestion/scripts/fdp_staging_loader.sh {1} {2} {3}'.format(
                            env, order_date, env, table_id))

                        ing_tab_task = BashOperator(task_id="Ingestion_" + ing_tab + "_" + env,
                                                    bash_command='sh -x /CTRLFW/FDP/{0}/ingestion/scripts/fdp_staging_loader.sh {1} {2} {3}'.format(
                                                        env, order_date, env, table_id), dag=dag,
                                                    execution_timeout=timedelta(hours=20))

                    if ing_tab not in tasks_dict:
                        tasks_dict[ing_tab] = ing_tab_task

                    tasks_dict[start_prod_name] >> tasks_dict[ing_tab] >> tasks_dict[country_service_name]
                tasks_dict[country_service_name] >> tasks_dict["dq_" + country_service_name] >> tasks_dict[product_name]


def setup_dependencies():
    for product, service_dict in product_services_ingestion_dict.items():
        start_prod_name = "start_" + product
        if product not in tasks_dict:
            prod_task = EmptyOperator(task_id='{0}_{1}'.format(product, env))
            tasks_dict[product] = prod_task
        if start_prod_name not in tasks_dict:
            start_prod_task = EmptyOperator(task_id='{0}_{1}_{2}'.format("start", product, env))
            tasks_dict[start_prod_name] = start_prod_task

    for product, service_dict in product_services_ingestion_dict.items():
        start_prod_name = "start_" + product
        if product not in tasks_dict:
            prod_task = EmptyOperator(task_id='{0}_{1}'.format(product, env))
            tasks_dict[product] = prod_task
        if start_prod_name not in tasks_dict:
            start_prod_task = EmptyOperator(task_id='{0}_{1}_{2}'.format("start", product, env))
            tasks_dict[start_prod_name] = start_prod_task
        for service, ingestion_str in service_dict.items():
            for ingestion_tab in ingestion_str.split(","):
                if ingestion_tab in services_set:
                    tasks_dict[ingestion_tab] >> tasks_dict[service]
                if ingestion_tab in products_set:
                    tasks_dict[ingestion_tab] >> tasks_dict[service]
                else:
                    tasks_dict[start_prod_name] >> tasks_dict[ingestion_tab] >> tasks_dict[service]
            tasks_dict[service] >> tasks_dict["dq_" + service] >> tasks_dict[product]

    """for service, prod in serv_to_prod_dict.items():
   if prod not in tasks_dict :
     prod_task = EmptyOperator(task_id = '{0}_{1}'.format(prod, env))
     tasks_dict[prod] = prod_task
   tasks_dict[service] >> tasks_dict[prod]
"""

# setup_dependencies()


global dag

with DAG(
        dag_id='fdp_products_dag_jan_29_uat_refresh_' + env,
        schedule_interval=None,
        start_date=pendulum.datetime(2022, 11, 29, tz="UTC"),
        catchup=False,
        dagrun_timeout=datetime.timedelta(hours=20),
        tags=['products_dag', 'product'],
        params={"order_date": Param(default='2022-09-30', type='string', minLength=2, maxLength=10)}
) as dag:
    update_params()
    build_serv_to_prod_dict()
    create_ing_tasks()
    create_service_tasks()
    setup_dependencies()
    build_country_specific_dependencies()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    dag.cli()
